The new factory's groundnut shell oil was opened at a price of 4 jiao and 8 fen for 3,500 dan yesterday. Tongchang groundnut shell oil was 5 jiao and 3 fen, with hundreds of dan opened. The above were all purchased by this street, and the market was stable.

Industry Sets Price for Cypress Wax 218

The Cypress Wax Industry Association received a telegram from Hankou stating that transportation is difficult and supply is dwindling. In addition, demand from various regions is strong. However, the industry of pressing wax in Macheng has set a price, notifying the industry to abide by it uniformly. The selling price is as follows: Heavy Jing 22 taels, Miscellaneous Heavy 21 taels and 8 qian, Macheng 21 taels, Inserted and Flat Jing are both 21 taels and 2 qian.

Metal White Lead Sheet Demand Exceeds Supply 219

Transactions of white lead sheets are very smooth, so the number of sheets opened is extraordinarily impressive. However, the arrival of goods is very small, so the market has a shortage of supply. Standards are increasing step by step. The current market price for No. 2 sheets can be estimated at 27 taels and 5 qian, No. 3 sheets at 25 taels, No. 4 sheets at 24 taels and 5 qian, No. 5 and No. 6 sheets are both 24 taels, No. 7 sheets at 23 taels and 5 qian, No. 8 sheets at 23 taels, and No. 9 and No. 10 sheets at 23 taels and 2 qian and 5 fen. It is said that there were 40 to 50 barrels traded yesterday, purchased by tea merchants and Hankou merchants.

White Lead Wire Continues to Rise 220

Recently, due to the scramble for white lead wire by merchants from Xunyang and Hankou, the market supply cannot meet the demand. As a result, standards continue to rise. Yesterday, more than 2,000 dan were traded, and the price was 1 qian and 5 fen higher than before. For example, No. 1 to No. 6 account for 7 taels and 2 qian and 5 fen, No. 7 to No. 9 account for 2 liang, No. 10 and No. 11 account for 9 taels and 2 qian and 5 fen, No. 12 accounts for 9 taels and 5 qian, No. 13 accounts for 9 taels and 7 qian and 5 fen, No. 14 accounts for 10 taels, No. 15 accounts for 10 taels and 2 qian and 5 fen, and No. 16 accounts for 11 taels for fine patterns.

According to a telegram from London on the 4th, black iron sheet 3x6 per bundle of 13 sheets, 107 pounds to 11 pounds, white iron sheet 74 GAUGE per ton of 10 pounds and 10 shillings, tinplate 20x14 per box of 112 bundles, 100 pounds of 16 shillings and 10 and a half pence, tungsten (China) 9 shillings and 9 pence, antimony remains at 18 pounds per ton.

Coal: Kailuan Coal Prices Vary 221

The prices of Kailuan coal sold in the market recently vary between the company and the merchants. The reason is that the goods currently sold by the merchants are all orders placed last year when prices were low, while the large quantities currently sold by the company are based on this year's new market conditions, so they are higher. Therefore, the selling prices of the two parties cannot be consistent. For example, the prices made in the market yesterday were 8 taels and 3 qian for No. 1 coal dross and 7 taels and 8 qian for No. 2 coal dross, and 8 taels and 5 qian for Kailuan coal blocks, while the prices sold by the merchants were 1 qian, 2 qian, 3 qian, or 4 qian lower per ton.

Business Sutra (6)

Simple Identification Method for Woolen Cloth Quality 222

When purchasing woolen cloth for clothing: (1) Consider whether the material is durable and wearable. (2) What kind of material should be matched for what kind of clothing? For example, for lined robes or camel hair robes, it is best to choose dark brown patterned woolen cloth or solid-color and mixed-color Ward woolen cloth. Matching materials are easy, but selecting materials is difficult for laymen. If you want to buy patterned woolen cloth, the texture must be soft, and it is best to hold it up to the sky and see that there are very few holes. Ward woolen cloth must be double-sided, and the heavier the body, the better. Rub it with your fingers (using your thumb and forefinger). If it moves smoothly, it has more wool content. If it is stiff and does not move, it is mostly yarn. In general, for woolen cloth, a firm texture is good, and a loose and hard texture is bad. A firm texture is durable and does not shed hair for a long time. A loose texture easily generates hairballs and is not durable. Therefore, whether it is serge, patterned woolen cloth, Ward woolen cloth, gabardine, or other various woolen fabrics, a tight and firm texture is valuable. Experts look at goods by first examining this point. For plain serge, also look at the thickness of the pattern. A fine and dense pattern is better. For yuan gabardine, a clear grain and pure color are of the highest quality. Lihua dyeing and those with Western English “England Fruit” characters are guaranteed not to fade. Test with a drop of nitric acid water. If the color turns tiger yellow, it will also not fade. If it changes to another color, it will fade. However, this is limited to the dyeing of gabardine and Ward woolen cloth. Patterned woolen cloth, which is woven from mixed-color wool threads, is not subject to this rule because it is woven from three or four colors of wool thread, so it cannot change color. In the summer, if you want to make a single long gown, it is best to make patterned woolen cloth that is firm and light, or all-wool feather yarn for suits. Do not make ordinary mercerized striped feather yarn. Because summer gowns must be washed and ironed, rayon striped feather yarn will be damaged in no time. Once exposed to sunlight, it fades very quickly. Therefore, never be greedy for cheap prices and suffer losses. If you want something cheap, you can cut plain-colored feather yarn. As for plain serge that costs 7 or 8 jiao per foot, most of it is French goods. It will change color in no time and is not durable. Compared to Ward woolen cloth, at a ratio of one to three, it is better to buy raw wool or sesame-colored serge. In cold weather, you can buy melton or rotten paste wool, which is cheaper and very durable. It is much more durable than lower-grade cooked wool serge that costs 7 or 8 jiao per foot.

Free Talk

Su Xiaoxiao and Lady White Snake (2) 238

— Cao Juren

Let's look at these two stories in a complex way. This is a good comparison. Su Xiaoxiao lived a life of aesthetic hedonism. She was a typical modern woman; she was the Oriental Camille. Lady White Snake is the opposite. She is a virtuous wife, completely sacrificing herself for her husband. But Su Xiaoxiao takes herself as the center and spins the male world upside down; writers thousands of years later continue to support her. Lady White Snake takes her "husband" as "heaven", following her husband's lead. The husband treats her as a monster and a snake, covering her head with a bowl and suppressing her body with the Leifeng Pagoda, preventing her from being born. Since the Southern Song Dynasty, our Chinese ethical code has gradually become complete and meticulous. Why is Su Xiaoxiao treated with such tolerance, and Lady White Snake treated so harshly? Isn't this worth considering? Originally, the leisurely and enjoyable life of an agricultural society was monopolized by the aristocracy (royal family, ministers, etc.) and the landlord class. Under the doors of the aristocracy and landlords, there were staff members and scholars who helped them in their leisure activities. Although Su Xiaoxiao's life was not tolerated by ethical codes, it was precisely an object of enjoyment for the leisurely class. Confucius was even willing to see Nanzi, and the princes and grandsons were naturally willing to be overthrown by Su Xiaoxiao. The writers of Pucao had at least eight dous of talent, and each was a talented scholar; where there are talented scholars, there must be beautiful women, and Su Xiaoxiao is the best target for thousands of talented scholars! The talented scholars who hum "This is the place where jade was buried" can be seen on the lake embankment every day. Therefore, Su Xiaoxiao's life, although outside the ethical code of the literati and officials, was within the scope of the literati and officials and could stay there to add color to the lakes and mountains. As for Lady White Snake, she is Xu Xuan's housewife; as soon as the daughter-in-law enters the door, the mother-in-law is unhappy. Whenever the mother-in-law talks about her daughter-in-law, she always shakes her head and sighs, "Ever since that fox spirit from my family entered the door, my son has been listening to her pillow talk, and everything has changed!" So the east is that fairy is not good, and the west is that fairy is not good, forcing the son to abuse his daughter-in-law, which is what the old lady wants. Fellow students, don't think that we were born in the 20th century and received education. If you marry into a big family, it's good if there are no changes in the man's family in the first few years after entering the door. If there is any trouble, the father-in-law loses his job, the husband loses his job, and they all blame you as a jinx, cursing you every day, making you unable to live in peace. Women who faithfully do their duty as virtuous wives are destined to be "monsters" and have the fate of "snakes", which is truly unavoidable! In the window frame of a pharmacy on Simar Road in Shanghai, there sat a young man in a long gown and mandarin jacket. A big snake was entangled around his body, and the snake's head was a beauty; that was the best illustration of "women are snakes". An ethical teacher said: If my mother weren't a woman, I would have killed all women!!! Of course, Su Xiaoxiao will not be killed.

Lady White Snake is not afraid of Xu Xuan, but Xu Xuan has the bowl given to him by the Zen Master Fahai, covering her head, making her unable to move. What is this bowl? It is economic power. When Lady White Snake was pressed underground, Zen Master Fahai built the foundation of the pagoda, and many people were willing to do good deeds and build a huge Leifeng Pagoda. This huge Leifeng Pagoda is the traditional thinking of thousands of years. "Economic power" and "traditional thinking" have crushed all women. Now that the Leifeng Pagoda has collapsed, Lady White Snake, who has emerged, still has the bowl of Zen Master Fahai covering her head. Can she move? Who will break this bowl for Lady White Snake? Students, please think carefully! (End)

A Certain Kind of People 239

— Li Bing

In China, a certain kind of people seem to exist solely to sigh, just like another kind of people exist solely for enjoyment.

When the revolutionaries drove away the boy Puyi, cut off the queue brought by the "Manchus", and replaced the dragon flag with the five-color flag, the sighs of a certain kind of people were noisy for a while.

As time passed, people gradually got used to the "bald head" life. Changing the emperor to the president did not seem to do them any harm. It should have been quiet, but civil wars started, taxes increased, and life became more difficult. Therefore, the people who "live to sigh" sighed long and short for this and that. The sound was no different from when the "emperor" was driven away.

Until the year before last, "national disasters" came again. First, there was a major flood disaster across the country. Secondly, the three northeastern provinces were occupied by Japan. Thirdly, a corner of Shanghai was destroyed. The government was at a loss, and naturally this was another excellent opportunity for people who "live to sigh" to stretch their necks and sigh. So, a long sound, a short sound, a sigh, and a huff echoed each other. That gloomy, hopeless sound was still the traditional set of twenty-three years ago!

When a person feels pain and is dissatisfied with reality, he should have the courage to take revenge and the power to transform. Taking a step back, he should also have solemn and righteous criticism and judgment. Taking another step back, harsh sarcasm and humorous satire are still the actions of living people. Only that gloomy sigh expresses despair and disillusionment!

A person who firmly grasps life has no time to sigh for himself. No matter how difficult, no matter how disastrous, no matter how oppressed, he can only keep fighting and be responsible for his own life. Sighing is a pathetic act of expressing that he has no grasp of his own life, it is the groan of a ghost, and the wail of a phantom.

However, the groans of ghosts and the wails of phantoms at least show that this era is not a "daytime" illuminated by sunshine, but a dark "night of death". Then, let us let this gloomy groan and the dark night of death pass together!

Humble Feelings After Reading the "Special Issue on the Lexical Liberation Movement" 240

— Yang Qiu

On the afternoon of the 5th of this month, I happened to pass by the place of my "friend" Li Liewen and accidentally saw the "Special Issue on the Lexical Liberation Movement" of his New Era (1) monthly magazine on his desk. I thought that since the poem liberation movement had already allowed our (not "my friend's") old Dr. Hu to enjoy his fame in our country for more than ten years, then the lexical liberation movement would certainly not be "very rigid", let alone this being a "special issue", which is naturally more "Young men and women, must read," and after reading it, there will be "unexpected effects." So I made up my mind to specifically ask my "friend" Li Liewen for this "special issue" and take it back to read with "my wife, Ms. XX." My "friend" Li Liewen was generous after all. The "special issue" was obtained immediately, so I took it back happily, burned three incense sticks, brewed two bowls of Longjing tea, solemnly opened the "special issue," and began to read it seriously, singing along with my wife.

After all, the "liberated lyrics" and the "unliberated lyrics" are "very different," just as women's liberated feet and unliberated three-inch golden lilies are very different. My wife, Ms. XX, and I read it piece by piece, and we read Mr. Zeng XX's "extremely wonderful words." Mr. Zeng XX is the "founder of the lexical liberation movement," the founder's "lyrics,"!! No, the "liberated lyrics," are especially "very different." After my wife, Ms. XX, read and burst into tears of joy, she insisted that I "publicize it widely," and I also felt that this good deed should not be missed, so I washed my hands and added incense and specially transcribed it respectfully. Look, here is it:

Painting Hall Spring

The day starts long at the beginning of the year, guests come to comfort my desolation.

It doesn't matter if you occasionally pass the time, just play mahjong.

Drink all the wine in the glass, who cares about national affairs?

Fortunately, there are beauties in front of the wine vessel, but you can't be crazy.

Divination Ballad

The Northeast is severely cold, not as warm as Jiangnan;

The puppet state actually sees peace, how is it like the chaos in the Central Plains?

The "plenary meeting" was also held, but saving the country became a hanging case;

All the attending gentlemen got official positions, but no one cares about the national crisis.

One good deed has been done, and we continued to read on. Surprisingly, "things in the world are never unique," and we also discovered the "genius poetry" of a "genius" Shao. Naturally, this good deed is even more not to be missed. Without waiting for my wife's request, I automatically washed my hands again and respectfully transcribed the following:

Inscription on Liu Haisu's "Autumn Sunset"

On the afternoon of December 17, 1932, I visited the contemporary painter Mr. Liu Haisu at Songyun Villa. I was captivated at first sight and talked very happily. Mr. Liu praised Yu very much at the time, praising Yu with the word "genius," which I have been grateful for for a long time. I have been wandering around the world for many years, and I have been a down-and-out scholar. There are many who admire Yu, but few who understand Yu. Today I met Haisu, and I realized that I had met a confidant. The sympathy of artists is very different from that of ordinary people. After saying goodbye, I was exceptionally happy. The next day, I remembered Haisu's painting "Autumn Sunset" and took up my pen to inscribe it. Haisu read it, what do you think?

The red sun has a long face in the sky,

Pressing down on the shaking branches.

The river is like a coffin standing still.

The red sun becomes like a cloudy Mask,

The valley is like a bird at dusk,

Silently dragging a sigh.

Now that two good deeds have been done, I felt at ease and content. My wife suddenly exclaimed "Oh dear!" I asked, "Oh dear," what is it? She said: "You have done two good deeds, but you have harmed the typesetting workers for nothing, and you have also ruined such good paper. You are wasting things, and this sin is not small!" After she said this, I couldn't help but stick out my tongue in shock, so I spoke a slogan to record my fault. The poem says:

Amitabha Buddha is above, I am doing things really absurd!

People have long days, and they should pass the time by playing mahjong;

People don't have beauties in front of the wine vessel, who cares whether they can be crazy?

The river stands still like a coffin, the red sun becomes like a cloudy paste,

Haisu also praised him as a "genius," who dares to say that it is "not very similar"?

"The Times" is new, but you are old-fashioned, who cares, who cares!

Copying wonderful sentences is still forgivable, but harming the workers is wrong;

Harming the workers is still forgivable, but wasting paper is a loss of conscience!

Amitabha Buddha is above, I will never be absurd again.

Various Things After the Death of Galsworthy 241

— Zhen

According to Reuters news, the late British writer Galsworthy may have a state funeral held at Westminster Abbey in London. Although this is still a proposal, it can already be seen how the British view writers. Many of Galsworthy's friends, of course, are all well-known contemporary writers, and are now jointly requesting the authorities to approve this request. It seems that the authorities will not refuse.

Galsworthy also had a will when he was critically ill, which was to have his body cremated. His wife received a condolence telegram from the Emperor and Queen from Sandringham Palace the day after his death, saying that the Queen and her wife were deeply saddened by the news of his death and expressed their sincere sympathy to Mrs. Galsworthy. They deeply felt that Galsworthy's death was a great loss to the literary world, and the British people, both at home and abroad, would feel grief.

Prime Minister MacDonald also had a condolence telegram: "Please allow me to offer my deepest sympathy. His death is a permanently unfillable hole in the world of literature."

Two days before Galsworthy was critically ill, he finished the last chapter of the trilogy he wrote after "Maid" and "Flowering Wilderness," with a manuscript of about 100,000 words. Although it was all a first draft, people who knew Galsworthy's writing style knew that Galsworthy was so meticulous when writing that even the first draft did not require much revision. However, these drafts can only be seen by his closest relatives and friends. According to an employee of Heinemann Bookstore, which publishes most of his works: "Galsworthy's first draft is as exquisite as other writers' revised drafts."

As for the Nobel Prize for Literature that Galsworthy recently received, the amount is 9,600 pounds. According to Galsworthy's wishes, he wants to give it all to the PEN Club for safekeeping. If the PEN Club stops, it will be changed to the Royal Literary Society Fund. The PEN Club is a gathering of writers from all over the world, and Galsworthy himself is still the chairman.

Love at the Crossroads of the Times (Manuscript Continued) 242

— Zhang Ziping

He kept staring at Madam Ren's corner. He felt that tonight's Peizhen was particularly beautiful. This was not only because her clothes were fashionable, but also because her inherent posture was moving. Her figure was light, and she stood tall and jade-like, with an elegant element in her beauty. He felt that she "Do you know her? Go ask her to dance with you."

Madam Hezi's voice could be heard with a bit of jealousy.

"Nonsense!"

He turned his head and smiled at her.

He saw Peizhen, still being embraced by that tall and fat man, walking out. At this moment, Haiquan desperately paid attention to what kind of person that big man was. The more he paid attention, the more he felt that the giant's face was vulgar and his face was also very dark. The five fingers that were resting on Peizhen's shoulders seemed to be as thick and clumsy as some sugarcane in Guangdong. Haiquan paid more attention to his feet, which was even worse. Although they were wrapped in suit pants, it could be imagined that they were heavy and inflexible. Only the words "elephant legs" could describe them. He thought that the giant's legs must be straight and without any distinction between the thighs, knees, and shins. "Why does Madam Ren associate with such a giant? This giant is undoubtedly a first-class figure in China, a warlord!"

He thought to himself, and sighed softly.

Twenty-four

Before eleven o'clock, they returned home.

After about two or three days of sunshine and warmth, the weather changed. When they came out of the dance hall, they felt an unexpected and fierce northerly wind.

"It must be snowing."

As soon as he stepped into the back door, he said this as if to himself. But she didn't answer him. He didn't know why she was so unhappy. From the moment she came out of the dance hall, she was silent and didn't say a word. Every time he asked her a question, she would only smile slightly and not answer. This made it a little difficult for him to deal with. When he went upstairs, he thought she would definitely follow him. But in the living room below, it seemed that two or three Japanese guests had come and were sitting in front of the fireplace with that Oriental guy, talking happily. Only that beautiful little girl, when she heard that they had returned, ran out as if flying. When she saw Haiquan, she smiled charmingly and bowed as usual.

When Madam Hezi saw that guests had arrived, she hurried to the front hall. She didn't say a word to him, waiting for him to come up to see him.

How to Be a Person? 243

— I

How to Be a Person?

This seems like a question that shouldn't be a question (last year, the editor of this publication, Mr. "Buddha," already spoke about it in detail), but to talk about it again might be very interesting.

People come in all shapes and sizes, and thus there are all sorts of rules for being a person, which are difficult to cover comprehensively. So, I will just briefly talk about how we people do it.

So, how are we doing it now? Very good. We respectfully follow the way of the sages and are worthy sons and grandsons of our great five-thousand-year-old ancient country. We would rather be so poor that we don't have food for three meals than become kidnappers. We would rather not have a single copper coin to buy a cigarette than pick up a cigarette butt on the street. We would rather be beaten black and blue by our wives, but it is not appropriate to openly flirt with other people's concubines. First, it is harmful to morality, and second, it is a matter of face. As for patriotism, we are even more serious. To show our determination not to buy inferior goods, we do not pass by the doors of such stores. To show our determination not to be slaves of a conquered nation, we glare at foreigners. Although this inevitably detracts from the gentlemanly demeanor, it is not a big deal.

However, upon careful consideration, it seems a bit wrong. After that, we can't help but start to doubt the way to conduct ourselves in the world. Of course, we must find another way. Although it is certainly unnecessary to become a robber or kidnapper, perhaps the principle of "small profits and quick turnover, sacrificing capital" in one's character might not be entirely impossible. So, we have to study the art of being a person in the future.

First, we have to get a conspicuous Western suit and learn a set of polite official phrases like "Thank you, thank you" and "You're too kind, you're too kind." Before high-ranking officials and nobles, we must be full of respect and reverence, congratulating them not only on their prosperous official career but also on how they benefit the country and its people. Before capitalists and landlords, in addition to not asking to borrow money or saying that they are rich and unkind, we must never show our own poverty and sourness. When their concubine celebrates her 20th birthday, even if it means using bandages for bound feet, we must send flower baskets or silver shields. If they go from Shanghai to Kunshan tomorrow, we must hold a banquet to see them off. If they go abroad, we must buy their boat tickets for them. When they write articles or give speeches, we must applaud and praise them. As for New Year's greetings and holiday visits, we must personally go to their door, which is the minimum requirement.

The above is for the big shots who are superior to us. As for the people whose economic status is below us, of course, we must put on an air of full of arrogance. When eating, there must be servants standing behind us; when taking a rickshaw, we must not haggle over the price; we must take first class on the tram; and when watching a play, we must go upstairs.

Thus, in this way, we will gradually squeeze into the upper class. Not only will it be no problem to watch racquetball and buy champagne tickets, but also in the autumn of national crisis when we "pacify the internal and then resist the external," in the time of "long-term resistance" and even "spiritual resistance," we might as well invent a kind of "eating to save the country," which will of course be a sensation. As for the business arena of actually selling out the country, why can't we take the opportunity to insert a foot in, using the philosophy that China is hopeless as an excuse?

Therefore, being a person is by no means difficult; it just depends on how earnestly you do it.

Petitioning and Asking for Leave 244

— Tan Yu

In the winter of the past year, students in Beiping braved wind and snow, lying on the rails to petition in Nanjing, demanding to send troops to resist Japan. Who didn't say they were enthusiastic and patriotic!

Now that the violent Japanese have occupied Yu Pass, and Tianjin and Peiping are in danger, this is precisely the time for them to petition. But the fact is exactly the opposite: they have asked for leave!

Alas! Enthusiasm! Patriotism! Is this the spirit of the Chinese nation! (Repaid) Science

The Evolution and Manufacturing of Light Bulbs 245

— Fan

Since Edison invented the light bulb, people all over the world have benefited from its light. However, when the light bulb was first invented, it used a lot of electricity, and the light was still dim. Only after many electrical scientists devoted themselves to hard work in the laboratory did we have today's light bulbs that are as bright as daylight.

Decades ago, our light bulbs were still very dim and yellowish. Because at that time, the filaments were made of carbon filaments, which were very expensive and not durable. Later, a metal called tungsten was invented for use as a filament, which was more energy-saving, brighter, and more durable than the previous carbon filaments. The commonly used long light bulbs on the market today are made of tungsten filaments. However, long light bulbs also have a shortcoming: because of the characteristics of tungsten filaments, they can secrete a gas after a long period of burning. This gas adheres to the light bulb, which is a yellowish substance. This yellowish substance can reduce the light and also detract from the appearance, so it is very annoying. Also, when this type of light bulb has been burning for a long time, the glass of the light bulb can transmit heat to the point where you can't put your hand on it, which is also one of the drawbacks.

We know that if we want the filament to glow, it must have a high temperature, so the inside of the light bulb is extremely hot, but we do not want the outside of the bulb to also generate high heat. So, another inventor came up with the idea of filling the light bulb with an inert gas, which had a significant effect: 1) The light bulb will not develop a yellowish substance after burning for a long time; 2) It will not transmit heat; 3) It saves more energy than tungsten filament lamps; 4) It is more durable than tungsten filament lamps. With these four major advantages, there is also a disadvantage: the price is more expensive than tungsten filament lamps. But compared to the advantages, the higher price is worth it. This lamp is originally called an inert gas lamp, but it is also called a Half lamp in the market, because "Half" means half, which means it can save half of the electricity.

Random Thoughts on the Year of the Abolished Lunar Calendar 246

— Jinmen

1.

Heaven is kind, and the weather has been sunny for days in the year of the abolished lunar calendar. All the cinemas and theaters are packed every day. The amusement parks are even more crowded. It can be said that people don't forget to have fun while saving the country. I think the owners of the amusement parks and theaters can make up for the losses they suffered last year during the "January 28th Incident" in one go this year.

2.

Our people's conservatism is unmatched by any other country. Even though the government has long adopted the Gregorian calendar, the people still outwardly comply but inwardly resist, and have not been able to firmly abolish the abolished lunar calendar. Even such a simple and easy thing is like this. No wonder we lag behind in everything. Alas!

3.

On the anniversary of the "January 28th Incident," various newspapers published a notice from the Citizens' Federation: "...All amusement parks and theaters will suspend entertainment for one day to commemorate the event..." However, very, very few people actually followed it. Most places were still as crowded as usual. Of course, the theater owners are making full house these days, so how could they be willing to sacrifice the profits of this one day! Alas!

4.

On the anniversary of the "January 28th Incident," many shops hung half-masts at their doors, but inside they were banging drums. I don't know if they were in sorrow or in joy. Such a contradiction is laughable.

The Way Out for Shop Assistants' Communications 247

Editor:

People living away from home, although there are various entertainment

Page 22

places to spend their spare time, and like-minded friends to be companions for entertainment. But, at a certain time, there is always an indescribable "boredom" in my heart. Sir! I am one of them.

I have been away from my hometown to Shanghai for only more than two months. Every day, my life, honestly, cannot be considered unsatisfactory. There are opportunities to increase knowledge, and there is a possibility of contacting society. I am also interested in the business I serve. And there is one day off every week, where I can do other proper entertainment to adjust the monotony of life. In theory, this environment is exactly what most people seek but cannot get, so there is nothing more to ask for, right? However, people's hearts are never satisfied. In this environment, I am yearning for the so-called "boredom of my peers"! I want to find a friend of the opposite sex to satisfy my desires.

But, I must solemnly declare: The so-called "desire" is not the mean and ugly "carnal desire," and it is not difficult to satisfy one's "carnal desire" in the evil Shanghai. What I want to solve is only the indescribable "boredom."

I am a married man, and I get along very well with my wife. Because the living standards in Shanghai are high and she has her own environment, I cannot resolutely bring her to Shanghai: so I want to find an ideal friend of the opposite sex. But I dare not, I am afraid of falling into the net of love and being unable to get out; I am afraid that my ideal friend of the opposite sex will be criticized by society and be in a dilemma. Because I know that the flames of young men and women are strong, and they can burn together at first contact; at the same time, I know that today's society is in a transition between the old and the new, and the new trends and the old morals are fighting. It is easy for a woman to make friends with a man and cause social misunderstandings, or even become a victim of the times. But I cannot relieve my "boredom." The contradictory psychology has been tossing in my chest for more than a day, and I can't find a solution. Sir! Please teach me! Thank you. Di Ji, 22, 2, 5.

Editor's note: After reading Mr. Di's letter, we firmly believe that Mr. Di's "desire" in his heart is indeed "not the mean and ugly carnal desire," but only to solve the indescribable boredom." But how can there be anything "unspeakable" in the world? We dare to assert that this "boredom" is of course somewhat related to "sex." Otherwise, after already having "like-minded friends as companions for entertainment," why must you find "a friend of the opposite sex to satisfy my desires"? We believe that this demand for "desire" is very natural, and everyone does not need to avoid it, like Mr. Di, hiding and covering up, saying something like "indescribable boredom." According to physiology, the nutrients used by an adult every day become two kinds of power, one is "kinetic energy" and the other is "potential energy." "Kinetic energy" is the energy we spend on doing things every day; "potential energy" is hidden in our limbs and officials, ready to reproduce. So, whether male or female, after reaching a certain age, this "potential energy" acts up, and they need a partner of the opposite sex to fulfill their innate reproductive obligations. However, when there is no opponent, this "potential energy" has no place to be used, and it becomes what Mr. Di calls "indescribable boredom."

Therefore, when "sexual desire" is not resolved, it is indeed inevitable to confuse "love," "affection," and "desire" when interacting too closely with friends of the opposite sex. As for the deviations and dangers after entering such a wrong path, Mr. Di said it clearly and unambiguously in his letter, so we don't need to dwell on it. We suggest that Mr. Di quickly strive in the economic field, break the environment, and bring his beloved wife to Shanghai to live together. At that time, if you go to make some friends of the opposite sex, we can agree, but now we advise you not to try it. This is also a way to remove the fuel from the stove!

A Family of Scholars (Continued from XIII) 249

— Wang Zhongxian

7. Sand Blew into Her Eyes

Living in the large kitchen were Ruohua, Youzhong, and Miss Daiqiu. This play of uncle and sister-in-law in love, of course, could not be hidden from Daiqiu. When Daiqiu saw it, she felt indescribably sad. Ruohua was her mother, and she couldn't protect her, she just hated Youzhong to the bone.

In the past, Daiqiu and Youzhong had the best feelings. She once said to him: "Why do I have to call you uncle? This is such a distant address! Wouldn't it be more intimate if I called you brother?"

Youzhong said to her: "When no one is listening, you can call me brother as much as you like. I am only twenty-three years old, and I am secretly willing to call you sister."

Youzhong often bought things to give her, and she also often hid from her mother and asked Youzhong to buy things. The two of them often hid in a room to talk, but no one knew what they were talking about.

Since discovering that Youzhong and her mother had immoral behavior, she had been sulking and refusing to eat. Her mother asked her why she didn't eat, and she said that she was seasick and had a headache; Youzhong asked her, and she pursed her lips all the way down to her chin. Youzhong avoided Ruohua's eyes and ears, and still like usual, went over to hold her hand, wanting to talk to her. She exerted herself to fling his hand away, turned her face to the window and looked at the turbulent sea.

"What are you angry about with me?" Youzhong asked gently.

Daiqiu ignored him a hundred times, and Youzhong kept asking. She drew a line downward with her palm, indicating that she was breaking off all relations with him. He still kept pestering her. So she resolutely replied:

"You are a dirty person. From now on, don't talk to me again! I'll pretend you're dead, and you pretend I'm dead!"

Hearing these words, which were more sour than pickled green plums, Youzhong's heart was as bright as if he had eaten fireflies. But, she was only a fifteen-year-old girl, how could she have such great jealousy? How could she understand the privacy of men and women? And also have the ambition to monopolize a handsome man? Probably the progress of the world is too fast, and the development of women is also particularly accelerated, and even underage girls know how to be jealous.

To say another word of conscience, Youzhong certainly never dreamed that his niece Daiqiu would fall in love with him. When they first met, she was only twelve years old, and it can be said that he watched her grow up. In these three years, he really loved her!! He hugged her willow-like waist, he kissed her apple-like cheeks! 丨However, these are definitely not expressions of erotic love. Everyone is happy to see a smart and beautiful child, even the old uncles with beards, hugging a little girl of about ten years old, and the old ladies with bald heads kissing a child with just erupted teeth, no one will turn their head askew and think of the issue of sex. Youzhong's love for Daiqiu is also like this.
